        forward_bytes_to_webusb_host((const uint8_t *)buf, pos);
      }
    }
    pos = 0;
    return write_ok();
  }

  static inline uint32_t count_newlines(const char *s, uint32_t n) {
    uint32_t lines = 0;
    for (uint32_t i = 0; i < n; ++i)
      lines += (s[i] == '\n');
    return lines;
  }

  inline uint32_t current_buf_pos() const { return pos < valid ? pos : valid; }

  inline uint64_t current_byte_offset() const { return byte_offset_of_buf + current_buf_pos(); }

  inline uint32_t current_line() const { return line_of_buf + count_newlines(buf, current_buf_pos()); }

  _noinline bool read_errorf(const char *fmt, ...) {
    char msg[160];
    va_list ap;
    va_start(ap, fmt);
    vsnprintf(msg, sizeof(msg), fmt, ap);
    va_end(ap);
    printf("json read error: %s at line %lu (byte %llu)\n", msg, (unsigned long)current_line(),
           (unsigned long long)current_byte_offset());
    return false;
  }

  _noinline void note_integer_clamp(int64_t before, int64_t after, int64_t min_value, int64_t max_value) {
    if (!reading || before == after) return;
    const char *key = active_field_key ? active_field_key : "<unknown>";
    printf("json clamped integer field %s from %lld to %lld (range %lld..%lld)\n", key, (long long)before, (long long)after,
           (long long)min_value, (long long)max_value);
  }

  _noinline void note_integer_clamp_u64(uint64_t before, uint64_t after, uint64_t min_value, uint64_t max_value) {
    if (!reading || before == after) return;
    const char *key = active_field_key ? active_field_key : "<unknown>";
    printf("json clamped integer field %s from %llu to %llu (range %llu..%llu)\n", key, (unsigned long long)before,
           (unsigned long long)after, (unsigned long long)min_value, (unsigned long long)max_value);
  }

  static inline bool is_json_terminator(char c) {
    return c == 0 || isspace((unsigned char)c) || c == ',' || c == ']' || c == '}';
  }

  bool fill() {
    if (!reading) return true;
    byte_offset_of_buf += valid;
    line_of_buf += count_newlines(buf, valid);
    if (memory) {
      uint32_t remaining = (memory_pos < memory_length) ? (memory_length - memory_pos) : 0;
      uint32_t n = remaining < bufsize ? remaining : bufsize;
      if (n > 0) memcpy(buf, memory + memory_pos, n);
      if (n < bufsize) memset(buf + n, 0, bufsize - n);
      memory_pos += n;
      valid = n;
      eof = (n == 0);
      pos = 0;
      return true;
    }
    UINT n = 0;
    FRESULT fr = f_read(f, buf, bufsize, &n);
    if (fr != FR_OK) {
      memset(buf, 0, sizeof(buf));
      pos = 0;
      valid = 0;
      eof = true;
      return read_errorf("file read failed (%d)", (int)fr);
    }
    if (n <= 0) n = 0;
    valid = (uint32_t)n;
    eof = (valid == 0);
    memset(buf + n, 0, bufsize - n);
    pos = 0;
    return true;
  }

  inline void emit_ascii_char(char c) {
    if (memory_copying()) return;
    if (pos >= bufsize) flush();
    buf[pos++] = c;
  }

  void _noinline emit_trailing_comma_and_key(const char *key) {
    if (reading) return;
    if (trailing_comma) emit_ascii_char(',');
    trailing_comma = true;
    if (!depth) return;
    bool is_array = is_array_bitmask & 1;
    emit_ascii_char('\n');
    for (int i = 0; i < depth; ++i)
      emit_ascii_char(' ');
    if (!is_array) {
      emit_string(key);
      emit_ascii_char(':');
    }
  }

  _noinline void emit_ascii_string(const char *s) {
    while (*s)
      emit_ascii_char(*s++);
  }

  inline void emit_escape_char(char c) {
    emit_ascii_char('\\');
    emit_ascii_char(c);
  }

  inline void emit_unicode(unsigned char c) {
    emit_ascii_char('\\');
    emit_ascii_char('u');
    emit_ascii_char('0');
    emit_ascii_char('0');
    emit_ascii_char(hexdigits[(c >> 4) & 0xf]);
    emit_ascii_char(hexdigits[c & 0xf]);
  }

  inline void emit_char(char c) {
    switch (c) {
    case '"':
      emit_escape_char('"');
      break;
    case '\\':
      emit_escape_char('\\');
      break;
    case '\b':
      emit_escape_char('b');
      break;
    case '\f':
      emit_escape_char('f');
      break;
    case '\n':
      emit_escape_char('n');
      break;
    case '\r':
      emit_escape_char('r');
      break;
    case '\t':
      emit_escape_char('t');
      break;
    default:
      if ((unsigned char)c >= 32 && (unsigned char)c <= 126)
        emit_ascii_char(c);
      else
        emit_unicode((unsigned char)c);
      break;
    }
  }

  _noinline void emit_string(const char *s, const char *e = nullptr, char charoffset = 0) {
    if (!e && s) e = s + strlen(s);
    emit_ascii_char('"');
    while (s < e)
      emit_char(*s++ + charoffset);
    emit_ascii_char('"');
  }

  inline char peek() {
    if (reading && pos >= valid) {
      if (eof) return 0;
      if (!fill()) return 0;
    }
    return buf[pos];
  }
  inline void next() { pos++; }
  inline char get() {
    char c = peek();
    next();
    return c;
  }
  inline bool consume(char c) {
    if (peek() == c) {
      next();
      return true;
    }
    return false;
  }

  inline bool skip_ws() {
    if (!reading) return true;
    for (;;) {
      while (isspace((unsigned char)peek()))
        next();
      if (peek() != '/') break;
      next();
      if (peek() == '/') {
        while (peek() && peek() != '\n')
          next();
        continue;
      }
      if (peek() == '*') {
        next();
        for (;;) {
          char c = peek();
          if (!c) return read_errorf("unterminated block comment");
          next();
          if (c == '*' && peek() == '/') {
            next();
            break;
          }
        }
        continue;
      }
      return read_errorf("unexpected '/'");
    }
    return peek() != 0;
  }

  _noinline bool serialise(uint64_t &o) {
    if (memory_copying()) return copy_field(&o, sizeof(o));
    if (reading) {
      if (!skip_ws()) return read_errorf("unexpected end of file before integer");
      o = 0;
      char c = peek();
      if (!isdigit((unsigned char)c)) return read_errorf("expected integer");
      if (c == '0') {
        next();
        if (isdigit((unsigned char)peek())) return read_errorf("invalid leading zero in integer");
      } else {
        do {
          c = peek();
          o = o * 10 + (uint64_t)(c - '0');
          next();
        } while (isdigit((unsigned char)peek()));
      }
      if (!is_json_terminator(peek())) return read_errorf("invalid character after integer");
    } else {
      char buf[21];
      uint64_t i = o;
      if (i == 0) {
        emit_ascii_char('0');
        return true;
      }
      int pos = 0;
      while (i > 0 && pos < (int)sizeof(buf) - 1) {
        uint64_t nexti = i / 10;
        buf[pos++] = '0' + (i - nexti * 10);
        i = nexti;
      }
      while (pos > 0)
        emit_ascii_char(buf[--pos]);
    }
    return true;
  }

  _noinline bool serialise(int64_t &o) {
    if (memory_copying()) return copy_field(&o, sizeof(o));
    if (reading) {
      if (!skip_ws()) return read_errorf("unexpected end of file before integer");
      bool neg = consume('-');
      uint64_t u = 0;
      if (!serialise(u)) return false;
      o = neg ? -u : u;
    } else {
      uint64_t u = o;
      if (o < 0) {
        emit_ascii_char('-');
        u = -o;
      }
      if (!serialise(u)) return false;
    }
    return true;
  }

  _noinline bool serialise(float &f) {
    if (memory_copying()) return copy_field(&f, sizeof(f));
    if (reading) {
      if (!skip_ws()) return read_errorf("unexpected end of file before number");
      bool neg = false;
      if (peek() == '-') {
        neg = true;
        next();
      }
      double value = 0.0;
      int exponent10 = 0;
      if (!isdigit((unsigned char)peek())) return read_errorf("expected number");
      if (peek() == '0') {
        next();
        if (isdigit((unsigned char)peek())) return read_errorf("invalid leading zero in number");
      } else {
        do {
          value = value * 10.0 + (double)(get() - '0');
        } while (isdigit((unsigned char)peek()));
      }
      if (peek() == '.') {
        next();
        if (!isdigit((unsigned char)peek())) return read_errorf("expected digit after decimal point");
        do {
          value = value * 10.0 + (double)(get() - '0');
          exponent10--;
        } while (isdigit((unsigned char)peek()));
      }
      if (peek() == 'e' || peek() == 'E') {
        next();
        bool exp_neg = false;
        if (peek() == '+' || peek() == '-') exp_neg = (get() == '-');
        if (!isdigit((unsigned char)peek())) return read_errorf("expected exponent digits");
        int exponent = 0;
        do {
          exponent = exponent * 10 + (get() - '0');
          if (exponent > 100) exponent = 100;
        } while (isdigit((unsigned char)peek()));
        exponent10 += exp_neg ? -exponent : exponent;
      }
      if (!is_json_terminator(peek())) return read_errorf("invalid character after number");
      while (exponent10 > 0) {
        value *= 10.0;
        exponent10--;
      }
      while (exponent10 < 0) {
        value *= 0.1;
        exponent10++;
      }
      f = neg ? (float)-value : (float)value;
    } else {
      char buf[17];
      snprintf(buf, sizeof(buf), "%.9g", f);
      buf[16] = 0;
      emit_ascii_string(buf);
    }
    return true;
  }

  _noinline bool serialise(bool &b) {
    if (memory_copying()) return copy_field(&b, sizeof(b));
    if (reading) {
      if (!skip_ws()) return read_errorf("unexpected end of file before boolean");
      if (peek() == 't') {
        if (!consume('t') || !consume('r') || !consume('u') || !consume('e'))
          return read_errorf("invalid boolean literal");
        if (!is_json_terminator(peek())) return read_errorf("invalid character after boolean");
        b = true;
        return true;
      }
      if (peek() == 'f') {
        if (!consume('f') || !consume('a') || !consume('l') || !consume('s') || !consume('e'))
          return read_errorf("invalid boolean literal");
        if (!is_json_terminator(peek())) return read_errorf("invalid character after boolean");
        b = false;
        return true;
      }
      return read_errorf("expected boolean");
    } else {
      emit_ascii_string(b ? "true" : "false");
      return true;
    }
  }

  _noinline bool read_escaped_char(char &c) {
    switch (peek()) {
    case '"':
      c = '"';
      next();
      return true;
    case '\\':
      c = '\\';
      next();
      return true;
    case '/':
      c = '/';
      next();
      return true;
    case 'b':
      c = '\b';
      next();
      return true;
    case 'f':
      c = '\f';
      next();
      return true;
    case 'n':
      c = '\n';
      next();
      return true;
    case 'r':
      c = '\r';
      next();
      return true;
    case 't':
      c = '\t';
      next();
      return true;
    case 'u': {
      next();
      int codepoint = 0;
      for (int j = 0; j < 4; ++j) {
        int digit = hex_digit_value(peek());
        if (digit < 0) return read_errorf("expected hex digit in unicode escape");
        codepoint = (codepoint << 4) | digit;
        next();
      }
      c = (char)codepoint;
      return true;
    }
    case 0:
      return read_errorf("unexpected end of file in string escape");
    default:
      return read_errorf("invalid escape sequence in string");
    }
  }

  _noinline bool skip_string_body() {
    while (true) {
      char c = peek();
      if (!c) return read_errorf("unexpected end of file in string");
      if (c == '"') {
        next();
        return true;
      }
      if ((unsigned char)c < 0x20) return read_errorf("unescaped control character in string");
      if (c == '\\') {
        next();
        char ignored = 0;
        if (!read_escaped_char(ignored)) return false;
      } else {
        next();
      }
    }
  }

  _noinline bool serialise_string(char *s, int n) {
    if (memory_copying()) return copy_field(s, (uint32_t)n);
    if (reading) {
      if (!skip_ws()) return read_errorf("unexpected end of file before string");
      if (!consume('"')) return read_errorf("expected '\"' to start string");
      int i = 0;
      bool overflow = false;
      while (true) {
        char c = peek();
        if (!c) return read_errorf("unexpected end of file in string");
        if (c == '"') {
          next();
          s[i] = '\0';
          if (overflow) return read_errorf("string too long (max %d chars)", n - 1);
          return true;
        }
        if ((unsigned char)c < 0x20) return read_errorf("unescaped control character in string");
        if (c == '\\') {
          next();
          if (!read_escaped_char(c)) return false;
        } else {
          next();
        }
        if (i < n - 1)
          s[i++] = c;
        else
          overflow = true;
      }
    } else {
      emit_string(s);
      return true;
    }
  }

  template <int N> inline bool serialise(char (&s)[N]) { return serialise_string(s, N); }

  _noinline void emit_object(bool is_array) {
    assert(depth < 32);
    is_array_bitmask = (is_array_bitmask << 1) | (is_array ? 1 : 0);
    emit_char(is_array ? '[' : '{');
    depth++;
    trailing_comma = false;
  }

  _noinline void emit_end_object() {
    assert(depth > 0);
    depth--;
    bool is_array = is_array_bitmask & 1;
    is_array_bitmask >>= 1;
    if (is_array) {
      emit_ascii_char(']');
    } else {
      emit_ascii_char('\n');
      for (int i = 0; i < depth; ++i)
        emit_ascii_char(' ');
      emit_ascii_char('}');
    }
    trailing_comma = true;
  }

  _noinline bool end() { // nb: we do not close; since this object doesn't open either, we shouldn't close.
    bool ok = write_ok();
    if (!reading) {
      while (depth > 0)
        emit_end_object();
      ok = flush() && ok;
    }
    f = NULL;
    return ok;
  }

  _noinline bool skip_value() {
    if (!skip_ws()) return read_errorf("unexpected end of file before value");
    if (consume('{')) {
      if (!skip_ws()) return read_errorf("unexpected end of file in object");
      bool first = true;
      while (!consume('}')) {
        if (!first) {
          if (!consume(',')) return read_errorf("expected ',' between object fields");
          if (!skip_ws()) return read_errorf("unexpected end of file after ',' in object");
          if (consume('}')) return read_errorf("trailing ',' in object");
        }
        char keybuf[17];
        if (!serialise(keybuf)) return false;
        if (!skip_ws()) return read_errorf("unexpected end of file after object key");
        if (!consume(':')) return read_errorf("expected ':' after object key");
        if (!skip_value()) return false;
        if (!skip_ws()) return read_errorf("unexpected end of file in object");
        first = false;
      }
    } else if (consume('[')) {
      if (!skip_ws()) return read_errorf("unexpected end of file in array");
      bool first = true;
      while (!consume(']')) {
        if (!first) {
          if (!consume(',')) return read_errorf("expected ',' between array elements");
          if (!skip_ws()) return read_errorf("unexpected end of file after ',' in array");
          if (consume(']')) return read_errorf("trailing ',' in array");
        }
        if (!skip_value()) return false;
        if (!skip_ws()) return read_errorf("unexpected end of file in array");
        first = false;
      }
    } else if (consume('"')) {
      if (!skip_string_body()) return false;
    } else if (peek() == 't') {
      if (!consume('t') || !consume('r') || !consume('u') || !consume('e'))
        return read_errorf("invalid literal, expected true");
      if (!is_json_terminator(peek())) return read_errorf("invalid character after literal");
    } else if (peek() == 'f') {
      if (!consume('f') || !consume('a') || !consume('l') || !consume('s') || !consume('e'))
        return read_errorf("invalid literal, expected false");
      if (!is_json_terminator(peek())) return read_errorf("invalid character after literal");
    } else if (peek() == 'n') {
      if (!consume('n') || !consume('u') || !consume('l') || !consume('l'))
        return read_errorf("invalid literal, expected null");
      if (!is_json_terminator(peek())) return read_errorf("invalid character after literal");
    } else if (peek() == '-' || isdigit((unsigned char)peek())) {
      char c = peek();
      if (c == '-') next();
      if (!isdigit((unsigned char)peek())) return read_errorf("expected number");
      if (peek() == '0') {
        next();
        if (isdigit((unsigned char)peek())) return read_errorf("invalid leading zero in number");
      } else {
        do {
          next();
        } while (isdigit((unsigned char)peek()));
      }
      if (peek() == '.') {
        next();
        if (!isdigit((unsigned char)peek())) return read_errorf("expected digit after decimal point");
        do {
          next();
        } while (isdigit((unsigned char)peek()));
      }
      if (peek() == 'e' || peek() == 'E') {
        next();
        if (peek() == '+' || peek() == '-') next();
        if (!isdigit((unsigned char)peek())) return read_errorf("expected exponent digits");
        do {
          next();
        } while (isdigit((unsigned char)peek()));
      }
      if (!is_json_terminator(peek())) return read_errorf("invalid character after number");
    } else {
      return read_errorf("expected JSON value");
    }
    skip_ws(); // its ok to get to eof here.
    return true;
  }
};

/*
Primitive `serialise(...)` overloads.

These are the building blocks used by `FIELD(...)`. You can also write your own overloads for custom structs.
*/
static inline bool serialise(serialiser_t &s, int64_t &i) { return s.serialise(i); }
static inline bool serialise(serialiser_t &s, uint64_t &i) { return s.serialise(i); }

static inline bool serialise(serialiser_t &s, int64_t &i, int64_t min_value, int64_t max_value) {
  bool rv = s.serialise(i);
  if (!rv || !s.reading) return rv;
  if (min_value == 0 && max_value == 0) return true;
  int64_t before = i;
  if (i < min_value) i = min_value;
  if (i > max_value) i = max_value;
  s.note_integer_clamp(before, i, min_value, max_value);
  return true;
}

static inline bool serialise(serialiser_t &s, uint64_t &i, uint64_t min_value, uint64_t max_value) {
  bool rv = s.serialise(i);
  if (!rv || !s.reading) return rv;
  if (min_value == 0 && max_value == 0) return true;
  uint64_t before = i;
  if (i < min_value) i = min_value;
  if (i > max_value) i = max_value;
  s.note_integer_clamp_u64(before, i, min_value, max_value);
  return true;
}

template <typename T> static inline int64_t clamp_bound_to_i64(T value) {
  return (int64_t)value;
}

template <typename T> static inline uint64_t clamp_bound_to_u64(T value) {
  return value < (T)0 ? 0 : (uint64_t)value;
}

#if defined(__SIZEOF_LONG__) && __SIZEOF_LONG__ == 4
static inline bool serialise(serialiser_t &s, long &i32) {
  if (s.memory_copying()) return s.copy_field(&i32, sizeof(i32));
  int64_t i = i32;
  bool rv = s.serialise(i);
  i32 = i;
  return rv;
}

template <typename MinT, typename MaxT> static inline bool serialise(serialiser_t &s, long &i32, MinT min_value, MaxT max_value) {
  if (s.memory_copying()) return s.copy_field(&i32, sizeof(i32));
  int64_t i = i32;
  bool rv = serialise(s, i, clamp_bound_to_i64(min_value), clamp_bound_to_i64(max_value));
  if (rv) {
    if (i < LONG_MIN) i = LONG_MIN;
    if (i > LONG_MAX) i = LONG_MAX;
    i32 = (long)i;
  }
  return rv;
}
#endif

static inline bool serialise(serialiser_t &s, float &f) { return s.serialise(f); }

static inline bool serialise(serialiser_t &s, bool &b) { return s.serialise(b); }

template <int N> static inline bool serialise(serialiser_t &s, char (&str)[N]) { return s.serialise_string(str, N); }

static inline int serialise_base64_digit_value(char c) {
  if (c >= 'A' && c <= 'Z') return c - 'A';
  if (c >= 'a' && c <= 'z') return c - 'a' + 26;
  if (c >= '0' && c <= '9') return c - '0' + 52;
  if (c == '+') return 62;
  if (c == '/') return 63;
  return -1;
}

static inline bool serialise_base64_bytes(serialiser_t &s, uint8_t *data, int &length, int max_length) {
  if (s.memory_copying()) {
    if (!s.copy_field(&length, sizeof(length))) return false;
    if (length < 0 || length > max_length) {
      printf("memory copy serialiser error: base64 length %d out of range 0..%d\n", length, max_length);
      return false;
    }
    return s.copy_field(data, (uint32_t)length);
  }
  if (s.reading) {
    if (!s.skip_ws()) return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file before base64 string");
    if (!s.consume('"')) return s.read_errorf("expected '\"' to start base64 string");
    int out_pos = 0;
    while (true) {
      char c0 = s.peek();
      if (!c0) return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file in base64 string");
      if (c0 == '"') {
        s.next();
        length = out_pos;
        return true;
      }
      char c1 = 0, c2 = 0, c3 = 0;
      c0 = s.get();
      c1 = s.get();
      c2 = s.get();
      c3 = s.get();
      if (!c1 || !c2 || !c3) return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file in base64 quartet");
      int v0 = serialise_base64_digit_value(c0);
      int v1 = serialise_base64_digit_value(c1);
      if (v0 < 0 || v1 < 0) return s.read_errorf("invalid base64 character");
      if (c2 == '=' && c3 != '=') return s.read_errorf("invalid base64 padding");
      int v2 = (c2 == '=') ? 0 : serialise_base64_digit_value(c2);
      int v3 = (c3 == '=') ? 0 : serialise_base64_digit_value(c3);
      if ((c2 != '=' && v2 < 0) || (c3 != '=' && v3 < 0)) return s.read_errorf("invalid base64 character");
      if (out_pos >= max_length) return s.read_errorf("base64 decoded data too long (max %d bytes)", max_length);
      data[out_pos++] = (uint8_t)((v0 << 2) | (v1 >> 4));
      if (c2 != '=') {
        if (out_pos >= max_length) return s.read_errorf("base64 decoded data too long (max %d bytes)", max_length);
        data[out_pos++] = (uint8_t)((v1 << 4) | (v2 >> 2));
        if (c3 != '=') {
          if (out_pos >= max_length) return s.read_errorf("base64 decoded data too long (max %d bytes)", max_length);
          data[out_pos++] = (uint8_t)((v2 << 6) | v3);
        }
      } else if (c3 != '=') {
        return s.read_errorf("invalid base64 padding");
      }
      if (c2 == '=' || c3 == '=') {
        if (!s.consume('"')) return s.read_errorf("expected end of base64 string after padding");
        length = out_pos;
        return true;
      }
    }
  } else {
    static constexpr char base64_table[] = "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/";
    if (length < 0 || length > max_length) {
      printf("json write error: base64 length %d out of range 0..%d\n", length, max_length);
      return false;
    }
    s.emit_ascii_char('"');
    for (int i = 0; i < length; i += 3) {
      uint8_t v0 = data[i];
      uint8_t v1 = (i + 1 < length) ? data[i + 1] : 0;
      uint8_t v2 = (i + 2 < length) ? data[i + 2] : 0;
      s.emit_ascii_char(base64_table[(v0 >> 2) & 0x3f]);
      s.emit_ascii_char(base64_table[((v0 << 4) | (v1 >> 4)) & 0x3f]);
      s.emit_ascii_char((i + 1 < length) ? base64_table[((v1 << 2) | (v2 >> 6)) & 0x3f] : '=');
      s.emit_ascii_char((i + 2 < length) ? base64_table[v2 & 0x3f] : '=');
    }
    s.emit_ascii_char('"');
    return true;
  }
}

typedef bool (*serialise_elem_func_t)(serialiser_t &s, void *elem);
typedef void (*serialise_soa_func_t)(void *elem, int &i, bool reading);

static _noinline bool serialise_array(serialiser_t &s, void *arr, int n, int *length, int elem_size, serialise_elem_func_t fn,
                                     int inner_dimension_2d = 0) {

  int limit = n;
  if (!s.reading)
    s.emit_object(true);
  else {
    if (!s.skip_ws()) return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file before array");
    if (length) *length = n;
    if (!s.consume('[')) return s.read_errorf("expected '[' to start array");
  }
  if (length && *length < limit) limit = *length;
  for (int i = 0; i < n && i < limit; i++) {
    if (s.reading) {
      if (!s.skip_ws()) return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file in array");
      if (s.consume(']')) {
        if (length) *length = i;
        return true;
      }
      if (i && !s.consume(',')) {
        if (length) *length = i;
        return s.read_errorf("expected ',' between array elements");
      }
      if (i) {
        if (!s.skip_ws()) {
          if (length) *length = i;
          return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file after ',' in array");
        }
        if (s.consume(']')) {
          if (length) *length = i;
          return s.read_errorf("trailing ',' in array");
        }
      }
    } else if (i) {
      s.emit_ascii_char(',');
    }
    void *elem = (uint8_t *)arr + i * elem_size * (inner_dimension_2d ? inner_dimension_2d : 1);
    if (inner_dimension_2d) {
      if (!serialise_array(s, elem, inner_dimension_2d, nullptr, elem_size, fn, 0)) return false;
    } else {
      if (!fn(s, elem)) return false;
    }
  }
  if (s.reading) {
    if (!s.skip_ws()) return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file in array");
    if (!s.consume(']')) return s.read_errorf(n == limit ? "array has more elements than expected" : "expected ']' to end array");
    return true;
  }
  s.emit_end_object();
  return true;
}

static _noinline bool serialise_soa(serialiser_t &s, void *arr, int n, int elem_size, serialise_soa_func_t fn,
                                   int special_value_to_swap_with_zero = 0, int min_value = 0, int max_value = 0,
                                   int soft_limit = -1) {
  if (s.memory_copying()) {
    printf("memory copy serialiser error: FIELD_SOA is not supported for panel settings transfer\n");
    return false;
  }
  auto encode_value = [&](int v) {
    if (special_value_to_swap_with_zero) {
      if (v == special_value_to_swap_with_zero)
        v = 0;
      else if (v >= 0)
        v++;
    }
    return v;
  };
  auto decode_value = [&](int &v) {
    if (special_value_to_swap_with_zero) {
      if (v == 0)
        v = special_value_to_swap_with_zero;
      else if (v > 0)
        v--;
    }
    if ((min_value != 0 || max_value != 0) && (!special_value_to_swap_with_zero || v != special_value_to_swap_with_zero)) {
      int before = v;
      if (v < min_value) v = min_value;
      if (v > max_value) v = max_value;
      s.note_integer_clamp(before, v, min_value, max_value);
    }
  };
  auto read_encoded_value_at = [&](int index) {
    int v = 0;
    void *elem = (uint8_t *)arr + index * elem_size;
    fn(elem, v, false);
    return encode_value(v);
  };
  auto store_decoded_value_at = [&](int index, int v) {
    void *elem = (uint8_t *)arr + index * elem_size;
    fn(elem, v, true);
  };
  if (!s.reading) {
    s.emit_object(true);
    if (n <= 0) {
      s.emit_end_object();
      return true;
    }
    int active_n = n;
    if (soft_limit >= 0) {
      active_n = soft_limit;
      if (active_n < 0) active_n = 0;
      if (active_n > n) active_n = n;
    }
    int write_n = active_n < n ? active_n + 1 : n;
    int default_encoded_value = encode_value(special_value_to_swap_with_zero);
    auto write_encoded_value_at = [&](int index) {
      return index < active_n ? read_encoded_value_at(index) : default_encoded_value;
    };
    int last = special_value_to_swap_with_zero;
    int last_change = 0;
    for (int i = 0; i < write_n; ++i) {
      int v = write_encoded_value_at(i);
      if (v != last) {
        last_change = i;
        last = v;
      }
    }
    bool first = true;
    for (int i = 0; i <= last_change;) {
      int v = write_encoded_value_at(i);
      int run_count = 1;
      while (i + run_count <= last_change && write_encoded_value_at(i + run_count) == v)
        run_count++;
      if (run_count >= 3) {
        if (!first) s.emit_ascii_char(',');
        first = false;
        s.emit_ascii_char('[');
        if (!serialise(s, run_count)) return false;
        s.emit_ascii_char(',');
        if (!serialise(s, v)) return false;
        s.emit_ascii_char(']');
        i += run_count;
      } else {
        for (int j = 0; j < run_count; ++j) {
          if (!first) s.emit_ascii_char(',');
          first = false;
          if (!serialise(s, v)) return false;
          i++;
        }
      }
    }
    s.emit_end_object();
    return true;
  }
  if (!s.skip_ws()) return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file before array");
  if (!s.consume('[')) return s.read_errorf("expected '[' to start array");
  int i = 0;
  int last = special_value_to_swap_with_zero;
  bool first = true;
  while (i < n) {
    if (!s.skip_ws()) return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file in array");
    if (s.consume(']')) {
      for (; i < n; ++i) {
        store_decoded_value_at(i, last);
      }
      return true;
    }
    if (!first) {
      if (!s.consume(',')) return s.read_errorf("expected ',' between array elements");
      if (!s.skip_ws()) return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file after ',' in array");
      if (s.consume(']')) return s.read_errorf("trailing ',' in array");
    }
    first = false;
    if (s.consume('[')) {
      int run_count = 0;
      int run_value = last;
      if (!serialise(s, run_count)) return false;
      if (!s.skip_ws()) return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file in SOA run");
      if (!s.consume(',')) return s.read_errorf("expected ',' in SOA run");
      if (!serialise(s, run_value)) return false;
      if (!s.skip_ws()) return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file in SOA run");
      if (!s.consume(']')) return s.read_errorf("expected ']' to end SOA run");
      if (run_count <= 0) return s.read_errorf("SOA run count must be positive");
      if (run_count > n - i) return s.read_errorf("SOA run has more elements than expected");
      decode_value(run_value);
      last = run_value;
      for (int j = 0; j < run_count; ++j)
        store_decoded_value_at(i++, last);
    } else {
      if (!serialise(s, last)) return false;
      decode_value(last);
      store_decoded_value_at(i++, last);
    }
  }
  if (!s.skip_ws()) return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file in array");
  if (!s.consume(']')) return s.read_errorf("array has more elements than expected");
  return true;
}

template <typename T> static inline bool serialise_array_elem(serialiser_t &s, void *elem) { return serialise(s, *(T *)elem); }

// variable length array
template <typename T, int N, typename LT>
static inline bool serialise(serialiser_t &s, T (&arr)[N], LT &length, int inner_dimension_2d = 0) {
  if (s.memory_copying() && !s.copy_field(&length, sizeof(length))) return false;
  int len = (int)length;
  bool rv = serialise_array(s, arr, N, &len, sizeof(T), serialise_array_elem<T>, inner_dimension_2d);
  if (s.reading) length = (LT)len;
  return rv;
}

// fixed length array
template <typename T, int N> static inline bool serialise(serialiser_t &s, T (&arr)[N]) {
  int len = (int)N;
  bool rv = serialise_array(s, arr, N, &len, sizeof(T), serialise_array_elem<T>);
  return rv;
}

// fixed length 2d array
template <typename T, int N, int N_INNER> static inline bool serialise(serialiser_t &s, T (&arr)[N][N_INNER]) {
  int len = (int)N;
  bool rv = serialise_array(s, arr, N, &len, sizeof(T), serialise_array_elem<T>, N_INNER);
  return rv;
}

/*
## Field Macros And Higher-Level Helpers

Higher-level helpers for arrays, presets, and field declaration.

Panels usually only need the macros below:

  - `OBJECT_BEGIN(s)` / `OBJECT_END(s)` for an object
  - `SUB_OBJECT_BEGIN(s, "name")` / `SUB_OBJECT_END(s)` for nested objects
  - `FIELD("key", value)` for a single value
  - `FIELD_ARRAY("key", array, length)` for a variable-length fixed-capacity array
  - `FIELD_SOA("key", data, member, ...)` for a compact "one member across many structs" array
  - `FIELD_SOA_LIMIT("key", data, member, limit, ...)` for a FIELD_SOA array with a live-entry write limit
  - `FIELD_ARRAY_INT_TRIM("key", data, ...)` for a compact plain integer array

`FIELD(...)` lines are used inside the switch statement generated by `OBJECT_BEGIN(...)`. On save, fields are emitted in source
order. On load, unknown keys are skipped automatically, which is why versioned upgrades are practical.

Typical usage looks like:

```cpp
bool my_panel::on_serialise(serialiser_t &s, int version) {
  OBJECT_BEGIN(s);
  FIELD("pattern", pattern);
  FIELD_ARRAY("steps", steps, step_count);
  SUB_OBJECT_BEGIN(s, "meta");
    FIELD("swing", swing);
  SUB_OBJECT_END(s);
  OBJECT_END(s);
  return true;
}
```

`FIELD_SOA(...)` is useful when you want to serialise one integer member across a whole array of structs in a denser form.
`FIELD_SOA_LIMIT(...)` writes only a live prefix plus a default boundary value, while still loading old full-width arrays.
`FIELD_ARRAY_INT_TRIM(...)` uses the same compact integer-array machinery for a plain integer array:

```cpp
FIELD_SOA("vel", steps, velocity, -128);
FIELD_SOA_LIMIT("vel", notes, velocity, note_count, 0, 0, 127);
FIELD_ARRAY_INT_TRIM("step_end", step_note_end, 0, 0, MAX_NOTES);
```
*/
/*
### `FIELD_SOA(...)` / `FIELD_SOA_LIMIT(...)` / `FIELD_ARRAY_INT_TRIM(...)`

`FIELD_SOA(...)` is the specialised "dense array" form. It serialises one integer member across an array of structs, trims
repeated values at the tail, can encode interior runs of 3+ equal values as `[count,value]`, can optionally remap a sentinel
value through zero so the JSON stays compact, and can optionally clamp non-sentinel values on load. `FIELD_ARRAY_INT_TRIM(...)`
does the same for plain integer arrays. `FIELD_SOA_LIMIT(...)` writes only the live prefix and emits one default boundary value
when that is needed to keep the existing tail-fill semantics correct on load.
*/
typedef struct synth_preset_t synth_preset_t;
bool serialise(serialiser_t &s, synth_preset_t &o, int flags);

#define OBJECT_BEGIN(s)                                                                                                            \
  char keybuf[17];                                                                                                                 \
  bool _plinky_object_first = true;                                                                                                \
  if (!s.reading) {                                                                                                                \
    s.emit_object(false);                                                                                                          \
  } else {                                                                                                                         \
    if (!s.skip_ws()) return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file before object");                                                \
    if (!s.consume('{')) return s.read_errorf("expected '{' to start object");                                                     \
    if (!s.skip_ws()) return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file in object");                                                    \
  }                                                                                                                                \
  while (!s.reading || !s.consume('}')) {                                                                                          \
    if (s.reading) {                                                                                                               \
      if (!_plinky_object_first) {                                                                                                 \
        if (!s.consume(',')) return s.read_errorf("expected ',' between object fields");                                           \
        if (!s.skip_ws()) return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file after ',' in object");                                      \
        if (s.consume('}')) return s.read_errorf("trailing ',' in object");                                                        \
      }                                                                                                                            \
      if (!s.serialise(keybuf)) return false;                                                                                      \
      if (!s.skip_ws()) return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file after object key");                                           \
      if (!s.consume(':')) return s.read_errorf("expected ':' after object key");                                                  \
    }                                                                                                                              \
    switch (s.reading ? literal_hash_span(keybuf, keybuf + strlen(keybuf)) : 1) {                                                  \
    default:                                                                                                                       \
      /*printf("unknown key: %s\n", keybuf);*/                                                                                         \
      if (!s.skip_value()) return false;                                                                                           \
      break;                                                                                                                       \
    case 1:

#define OBJECT_END(s)                                                                                                               \
  } /* switch */                                                                                                                   \
  if (!s.reading) {                                                                                                                \
    s.emit_end_object(); break;                                                                                                           \
  } else {                                                                                                                         \
    if (!s.skip_ws()) return s.read_errorf("unexpected end of file in object");                                                    \
    _plinky_object_first = false;                                                                                                  \
  }                                                                                                                                \
  } /* while */

#define SUB_OBJECT_BEGIN(s, key)                                                                                                   \
  case (HASH(key)): {                                                                                                              \
    s.emit_trailing_comma_and_key(key);                                                                                            \
    OBJECT_BEGIN(s);
#define SUB_OBJECT_END(s)                                                                                                          \
  OBJECT_END(s);                                                                                                                   \
  }

#define FIELD_BREADCRUMB_CORE0(key) debug_breadcrumb_mark_core0(PROFILE_FOURCC(key "    "))

#define FIELD(key, ...)                                                                                                           \
  static_assert(sizeof(key) <= 16, "FIELD key must be shorter than 16 characters");                                              \
  case (HASH(key)):                                                                                                                \
    FIELD_BREADCRUMB_CORE0(key);                                                                                                   \
    s.emit_trailing_comma_and_key(key);                                                                                            \
    s.active_field_key = key;                                                                                                      \
    if (!serialise(s, __VA_ARGS__)) return false;                                                                                         \
    s.active_field_key = NULL;                                                                                                     \
    if (s.reading) break;

#define FIELD_ARRAY(key, data, length)                                                                                             \
  case (HASH(key)):                                                                                                                \
    FIELD_BREADCRUMB_CORE0(key);                                                                                                   \
    s.emit_trailing_comma_and_key(key);                                                                                            \
    if (!serialise(s, data, length)) return false;                                                                                 \
    if (s.reading) break;

/* `FIELD_FN(...)` lets callers provide custom serialisation logic for one named field. */
#define FIELD_FN(key, fn, ...)                                                                                                          \
  case (HASH(key)):                                                                                                                \
    FIELD_BREADCRUMB_CORE0(key);                                                                                                   \
    s.emit_trailing_comma_and_key(key);                                                                                            \
    if (!(fn(s, ##__VA_ARGS__ ))) return false;                                                                                                    \
    if (s.reading) break;

#define FIELD_BASE64(key, data, length, max_length)                                                                                \
  case (HASH(key)):                                                                                                                \
    FIELD_BREADCRUMB_CORE0(key);                                                                                                   \
    s.emit_trailing_comma_and_key(key);                                                                                            \
    s.active_field_key = key;                                                                                                      \
    if (!serialise_base64_bytes(s, (uint8_t *)(data), length, max_length)) return false;                                          \
    s.active_field_key = NULL;                                                                                                     \
    if (s.reading) break;

#define FIELD_SYNTH_PRESET(key, index) FIELD(key, o.synth_presets[index], SERIALISE_PRESET_INCLUDE_BANK_FILENAME)
#define FIELD_MIX_PRESET(key) FIELD(key, o.synth_presets[MIX_PRESET_IDX], SERIALISE_PRESET_INCLUDE_BANK_FILENAME | SERIALISE_PRESET_IS_MIX_PRESET)

/* `FIELD_SOA(...)` serialises one integer member of an array of structs in a compact "structure of arrays" style. */
#define FIELD_SOA(key, data, member, ...)                                                                                          \
  case (HASH(key)):                                                                                                                \
    s.emit_trailing_comma_and_key(key);                                                                                            \
    s.active_field_key = key;                                                                                                      \
    if (!serialise_soa(s, (void *)(data), (int)(sizeof(data) / sizeof((data)[0])), (int)sizeof((data)[0]),                         \
                       [](void *elem, int &i, bool reading) {                                                                      \
                         auto *d = static_cast<decltype(&(data)[0])>(elem);                                                        \
                         if (reading)                                                                                              \
                           d->member = i;                                                                                          \
                         else                                                                                                      \
                           i = d->member;                                                                                          \
                       } __VA_OPT__(, ) __VA_ARGS__))                                                                              \
      return false;                                                                                                                \
    s.active_field_key = NULL;                                                                                                     \
    if (s.reading) break;

/* `FIELD_SOA_LIMIT(...)` uses the FIELD_SOA format but ignores saved junk beyond `limit` on write. */
#define FIELD_SOA_LIMIT(key, data, member, limit, special_value_to_swap_with_zero, min_value, max_value)                           \
  case (HASH(key)):                                                                                                                \
    s.emit_trailing_comma_and_key(key);                                                                                            \
    s.active_field_key = key;                                                                                                      \
    if (!serialise_soa(s, (void *)(data), (int)(sizeof(data) / sizeof((data)[0])), (int)sizeof((data)[0]),                         \
                       [](void *elem, int &i, bool reading) {                                                                      \
                         auto *d = static_cast<decltype(&(data)[0])>(elem);                                                        \
                         if (reading)                                                                                              \
                           d->member = i;                                                                                          \
                         else                                                                                                      \
                           i = d->member;                                                                                          \
                       },                                                                                                          \
                       special_value_to_swap_with_zero, min_value, max_value, (int)(limit)))                                       \
      return false;                                                                                                                \
    s.active_field_key = NULL;                                                                                                     \
    if (s.reading) break;

/* `FIELD_ARRAY_INT_TRIM(...)` serialises a plain integer array using the same compact format as `FIELD_SOA(...)`. */
#define FIELD_ARRAY_INT_TRIM(key, data, ...)                                                                                       \
  case (HASH(key)):                                                                                                                \
    s.emit_trailing_comma_and_key(key);                                                                                            \
    s.active_field_key = key;                                                                                                      \
    if (!serialise_soa(s, (void *)(data), (int)(sizeof(data) / sizeof((data)[0])), (int)sizeof((data)[0]),                         \
                       [](void *elem, int &i, bool reading) {                                                                      \
                         auto *d = static_cast<decltype(&(data)[0])>(elem);                                                        \
                         if (reading)                                                                                              \
                           *d = i;                                                                                                 \
                         else                                                                                                      \
                           i = *d;                                                                                                 \
                       } __VA_OPT__(, ) __VA_ARGS__))                                                                              \
      return false;                                                                                                                \
    s.active_field_key = NULL;                                                                                                     \
    if (s.reading) break;

/* `FIELD_2D_COL(...)` serialises one column of a 2d array of ints */
#define FIELD_2D_COL(key, data, column_idx, ...)                                                                                          \
  case (HASH(key)):                                                                                                                \
    s.emit_trailing_comma_and_key(key);                                                                                            \
    if (!serialise_soa(s, (void *)(data), (int)(sizeof(data) / sizeof((data)[0])), (int)sizeof((data)[0]),                         \
                       [](void *elem, int &i, bool reading) {                                                                      \
                         auto *d = static_cast<decltype(&(data)[0][0])>(elem);                                                        \
                         if (reading)                                                                                              \
                           d[column_idx] = i;                                                                                          \
                         else                                                                                                      \
                           i = d[column_idx];                                                                                          \
                       } __VA_OPT__(, ) __VA_ARGS__))                                                                              \
      return false;                                                                                                                \
    if (s.reading) break;

===== blocks_ll.h =====

/*
# blocks_ll.h

`blocks_ll.h` is the low-level Plinky runtime API.

This file exposes the hardware-shaped view of the instrument: the 16x16 pressure grid, the LED framebuffer on the same grid, the
four side buttons, MIDI and CV ports, the global scroll/page position, and a handful of small runtime helpers.

Most panel authors should start with `blocks.h`, which builds higher-level widgets, transport helpers, playheads, synth helpers,
and save/load UI on top of this layer.

Use `blocks_ll.h` when you need raw access, when you are building your own abstractions, or when the higher-level helpers in
`blocks.h` intentionally hide too much detail.
*/

/*
## Core 0 Temp Scratch

`temp_alloc(...)` / `temp_free(...)` expose a 4k transient scratch arena intended for brief, large core 0 temporaries such as
preset snapshots, `FIL`, `serialiser_t`, and other working state that should not live on the core 0 stack.

Core 0 stack space is tight, so this arena exists to keep large temporaries off the stack when a short-lived scratch object is
needed.

For C++ code, the preferred API is:

  - `make_temp_object<T>(tag)` for one temporary object
  - `make_temp_array<T>(count, tag)` for a temporary array

These return a small RAII wrapper that calls `temp_free(...)` automatically on scope exit, including early returns.

Raw `temp_alloc(...)` / `temp_free(...)` are still the right interface for C code.

Rules:

  - core 0 only
  - strict LIFO: frees must exactly reverse the allocation order
  - brief lifetimes only; never store the returned pointer into persistent or cross-core state
  - keep ordinary small locals on the stack; use this for the large objects that would otherwise make stack usage risky

Violations trap even in release builds.
*/

void *temp_alloc(size_t size, size_t align, uint32_t tag);
void temp_free(void *ptr, uint32_t tag);

/*
## RGB PPM Loading

`read_rgb_ppm(...)` loads an 8-bit binary RGB PPM (`P6`, maxval 255) from the SD card.

On input, `*w` and `*h` must be positive and are treated as the maximum accepted width and height. On success, they are updated
to the true image width and height.

If `dest` is non-null, it must point to a buffer large enough for the maximum `w * h * 3` bytes. If `dest` is null, the function
uses the core-0 temp allocator and returns a buffer that must be released with `temp_free(ptr, READ_RGB_PPM_TEMP_TAG)`.

Returns the pixel buffer on success, or `NULL` on failure.
*/
#define READ_RGB_PPM_TEMP_TAG ((uint32_t)0x30504d50u) // "PPM0"
uint8_t *read_rgb_ppm(const char *filename, int *w, int *h, uint8_t *dest);

/*
## Convenience Math And Utility Helpers

This header also provides a handful of tiny inline helpers for common operations such as min/max, clamp, squaring, simple random
numbers, a few compact fixed-point utilities, and the DSP-safe `soft_clip(...)` / `hard_clip(...)` helpers. They are handy when
writing panel code, but the individual implementations are not especially interesting to read.
*/
static inline unsigned int maxu(unsigned int a, unsigned int b) { return a > b ? a : b; }

static inline int maxi(int a, int b) { return a > b ? a : b; }
static inline int mini(int a, int b) { return a < b ? a : b; }
static inline int clampi(int a, int b, int c) { return maxi(b, mini(a, c)); }
typedef struct stereo16_t {
  int16_t l, r;
} stereo16_t;
static inline stereo16_t make_stereo16(int l, int r) {
  stereo16_t v = {(int16_t)l, (int16_t)r};
  return v;
}
static inline stereo16_t clip_stereo16(int l, int r) {
  return make_stereo16(clampi(l, -32768, 32767), clampi(r, -32768, 32767));
}
static inline int squarei(int x) { return x * x; }
static inline float squaref(float x) { return (x * x); }
static inline uint32_t pcg_mix(uint32_t state) {
  uint32_t word = ((state >> ((state >> 28u) + 4u)) ^ state) * 277803737u;
  return (word >> 22u) ^ word;
}
static inline uint32_t pcg_next(uint32_t state) { return state * 747796405u + 2891336453u; }
static inline uint32_t pcg_hash(uint32_t input) { return pcg_mix(pcg_next(input)); }

static inline int update_ema(int current, int target, int smooth_shift) {
  int deadzone = 1<<smooth_shift;
  int delta = target-current;
  if (delta <= deadzone && delta >= -deadzone) return target;
  return current + (delta>>smooth_shift);
}

static inline int lerpi(int a, int b, int t_q8) { return a + (((b - a) * t_q8) >> 8); }
static inline float lerpf(float a, float b, float t) { return a + (b - a) * t; }
static inline int remapi(int x, int in_min, int in_max, int out_min, int out_max) {
  if (in_max == in_min) return out_min;
  x = clampi(x, mini(in_min, in_max), maxi(in_min, in_max));
  int out = out_min + ((x - in_min) * (out_max - out_min)) / (in_max - in_min);
  return clampi(out, mini(out_min, out_max), maxi(out_min, out_max));
}

static inline float clampf(float x, float a, float b) { return x < a ? a : x > b ? b : x; }
static inline float maxf(float a, float b) { return a > b ? a : b; }
static inline float minf(float a, float b) { return a < b ? a : b; }


static inline int count_bits(uint32_t x) { return __builtin_popcount(x); }
static inline int count_leading_zeros(uint32_t x) { return __builtin_clz(x); }  // undefined for 0
static inline int count_trailing_zeros(uint32_t x) { return __builtin_ctz(x); } // undefined for 0

static inline int make_lpf_delta(
    int target, int current,
    int speed_shift) { // ensure rounding means we always 'get there' in the end. effectively this is 'round to +- infinity' :)
  int delta = (target - current);
  if (delta > 0) delta += (1 << speed_shift) - 1;
  return delta >> speed_shift;
}

static inline int randi(int min, int max) { // inclusive
  if (min >= max) return min;
  return min + (rand() % (max - min + 1));
}

static inline void strncpy_safe(char *dst, const char *src, size_t n) {
  if (n < 1) return;
  size_t srclen = strlen(src) + 1;
  if (srclen >= n) srclen = n;
  memcpy(dst, src, srclen);
  dst[n - 1] = 0;
}

static inline int atan2i_q16(int y, int x) { // like atan2, but uses a square instead of a circle, and 16 bit fixed point. -32768 to 32768 output instead of -pi to pi.
  int ax = abs(x), ay = abs(y);
  if (ax >= ay) {
    if (ax == 0) return 0;
    int sy = (y*8192)/ax; // 8192 is 'pi/4'
    return (x>=0) ? sy : (y>0) ? 32768-sy : -32768-sy; // 32768 is 'pi'
  } else {
    int sx = (x*8192)/ay; // 8192 is 'pi/4'
    return (y>=0) ? 16384-sx : sx-16384; // 16384 is 'pi/2'
  }
}

extern const int16_t sin_table_q15[256];
extern const uint16_t sqrt_tab_q11[1024];
extern const int16_t wavetable[][16384];
static inline int16_t sin_table_interp_q15(uint32_t phase_q24) {
  uint32_t pos = (phase_q24 >> 24) & 255;
  int frac = (phase_q24 >> 8) & 65535;
  int p0 = sin_table_q15[pos];
  int p1 = sin_table_q15[(pos + 1) & 255];
  return p0 + (((p1 - p0) * frac) >> 16);
}
static inline int16_t wavetable_interp_q15(uint32_t phase_q24, uint32_t shape_q16) {
  uint32_t pos = (phase_q24 >> 23) & 511u;
  int frac = (phase_q24 >> 7) & 65535;
  uint32_t base = shape_q16 & 65535u;
  uint32_t idx0 = (base + pos) & 65535u;
  uint32_t idx1 = (idx0 + 1) & 65535u;
  int p0 = wavetable[idx0 >> 14][idx0 & 16383];
  int p1 = wavetable[idx1 >> 14][idx1 & 16383];
  return p0 + (((p1 - p0) * frac) >> 16);
}
static inline int soft_clip(int s_q15);
static inline int hard_clip(int s_q15);

/*
## Biquad Helpers

Small direct-form-II-transposed biquad helpers for panel DSP. Coefficients use normalized RBJ cookbook form:
`fb0..fb2` are the feed-forward coefficients and `fa1..fa2` are the denominator coefficients used by
`y = fb0*x + z1; z1 = fb1*x - fa1*y + z2; z2 = fb2*x - fa2*y`.
*/
typedef struct biquad_coeff_t {
  float fb0, fb1, fb2, fa1, fa2;
} biquad_coeff_t;

typedef struct biquad_t {
  float fz1, fz2;
} biquad_t;

typedef enum biquad_rbj_filter_t {
  BIQUAD_RBJ_LOWPASS,
  BIQUAD_RBJ_HIGHPASS,
  BIQUAD_RBJ_BANDPASS,
} biquad_rbj_filter_t;

static inline biquad_coeff_t biquad_coeff_make(float fb0, float fb1, float fb2, float fa1, float fa2) {
  biquad_coeff_t c = {fb0, fb1, fb2, fa1, fa2};
  return c;
}
static inline biquad_coeff_t biquad_coeff_make_bypass(void) { return biquad_coeff_make(1.f, 0.f, 0.f, 0.f, 0.f); }
static inline biquad_coeff_t biquad_coeff_make_unit_delay(void) { return biquad_coeff_make(0.f, 1.f, 0.f, 0.f, 0.f); }
static inline void biquad_coeff_set(biquad_coeff_t *c, float fb0, float fb1, float fb2, float fa1, float fa2) {
  *c = biquad_coeff_make(fb0, fb1, fb2, fa1, fa2);
}
static inline void biquad_coeff_set_bypass(biquad_coeff_t *c) { *c = biquad_coeff_make_bypass(); }
static inline void biquad_reset(biquad_t *b) { b->fz1 = b->fz2 = 0.f; }
static inline void biquad_coeff_set_normalized(biquad_coeff_t *c, float b0, float b1, float b2, float a0, float a1, float a2) {
  float inv_a0 = a0 != 0.f ? 1.f / a0 : 1.f;
  biquad_coeff_set(c, b0 * inv_a0, b1 * inv_a0, b2 * inv_a0, a1 * inv_a0, a2 * inv_a0);
}

/*
### RBJ Biquads

These helpers use the bilinear half-angle parameter

  g = tan(w / 2) = tan(pi * cutoff_hz / sample_rate)

instead of `cutoff_hz`. This is the usual trapezoidal/SVF cutoff variable. It is monotonic from 0 to infinity as cutoff moves
from DC to Nyquist, and it lets callers shape a musical sweep directly without converting through log-frequency hertz or calling
trig in the audio path.

For RBJ coefficients, `g` gives the needed sine/cosine terms by rational identities:

  sin(w) = 2g / (1 + g*g)
  cos(w) = (1 - g*g) / (1 + g*g)

Callers should clamp or table-map `g` to a finite useful range. Values near zero put the cutoff near DC; very large values put it
near Nyquist.
*/
static inline void biquad_coeff_set_rbj(biquad_coeff_t *c, biquad_rbj_filter_t type, float cutoff_g, float q) {
  cutoff_g = clampf(cutoff_g, 0.000001f, 64.f);
  q = maxf(q, 0.001f);
  float g2 = cutoff_g * cutoff_g;
  float inv = 1.f / (1.f + g2);
  float cw = (1.f - g2) * inv;
  float sw = 2.f * cutoff_g * inv;
  float a = sw / (2.f * q);
  if (type == BIQUAD_RBJ_LOWPASS)
    biquad_coeff_set_normalized(c, (1.f - cw) * 0.5f, 1.f - cw, (1.f - cw) * 0.5f, 1.f + a, -2.f * cw, 1.f - a);
  else if (type == BIQUAD_RBJ_HIGHPASS)
    biquad_coeff_set_normalized(c, (1.f + cw) * 0.5f, -(1.f + cw), (1.f + cw) * 0.5f, 1.f + a, -2.f * cw, 1.f - a);
  else
    biquad_coeff_set_normalized(c, sw * 0.5f, 0.f, -sw * 0.5f, 1.f + a, -2.f * cw, 1.f - a);
}
static inline void biquad_coeff_set_rbj_lowpass(biquad_coeff_t *c, float cutoff_g, float q) {
  biquad_coeff_set_rbj(c, BIQUAD_RBJ_LOWPASS, cutoff_g, q);
}
static inline void biquad_coeff_set_rbj_highpass(biquad_coeff_t *c, float cutoff_g, float q) {
  biquad_coeff_set_rbj(c, BIQUAD_RBJ_HIGHPASS, cutoff_g, q);
}
static inline void biquad_coeff_set_rbj_bandpass(biquad_coeff_t *c, float cutoff_g, float q) {
  biquad_coeff_set_rbj(c, BIQUAD_RBJ_BANDPASS, cutoff_g, q);
}

static const float biquad_coeff_default_g_table[] = {
    0.006283268f, 0.014f, 0.032f, 0.075f, 0.17f, 0.38f, 0.8f, 1.3f, 2.f};

static inline float biquad_coeff_interp_g_table(float t) {
  const int count = (int)(sizeof(biquad_coeff_default_g_table) / sizeof(biquad_coeff_default_g_table[0]));
  t = clampf(t, 0.f, 1.f);
  float pos = t * (float)(count - 1);
  int idx = (int)pos;
  if (idx >= count - 1)
    return biquad_coeff_default_g_table[count - 1];
  float frac = pos - (float)idx;
  return biquad_coeff_default_g_table[idx] + (biquad_coeff_default_g_table[idx + 1] - biquad_coeff_default_g_table[idx]) * frac;
}
static inline biquad_coeff_t biquad_coeff_make_dj_filter(int filter) {
  int d = clampi(filter, -127, 127);
  int mag = abs(d);
  const int bypass_mag = 20;
  if (mag <= bypass_mag) return biquad_coeff_make_unit_delay();
  int t_num = mag - bypass_mag;
  int t_den = 127 - bypass_mag;
  float t = (float)t_num / (float)t_den;
  float cutoff_g = biquad_coeff_interp_g_table(d < 0 ? 1.f - t : t);
  biquad_coeff_t c;
  biquad_coeff_set_rbj(&c, d < 0 ? BIQUAD_RBJ_LOWPASS : BIQUAD_RBJ_HIGHPASS, cutoff_g, 0.85f);
  return c;
}
static inline biquad_coeff_t biquad_coeff_add(biquad_coeff_t a, biquad_coeff_t b) {
  return biquad_coeff_make(a.fb0 + b.fb0, a.fb1 + b.fb1, a.fb2 + b.fb2, a.fa1 + b.fa1, a.fa2 + b.fa2);
}
static inline biquad_coeff_t biquad_coeff_diff(biquad_coeff_t a, biquad_coeff_t b) {
  return biquad_coeff_make(a.fb0 - b.fb0, a.fb1 - b.fb1, a.fb2 - b.fb2, a.fa1 - b.fa1, a.fa2 - b.fa2);
}
static inline biquad_coeff_t biquad_coeff_mul(biquad_coeff_t c, float x) {
  return biquad_coeff_make(c.fb0 * x, c.fb1 * x, c.fb2 * x, c.fa1 * x, c.fa2 * x);
}
static inline void biquad_coeff_accum(biquad_coeff_t *a, biquad_coeff_t b) { *a = biquad_coeff_add(*a, b); }
static inline biquad_coeff_t biquad_coeff_lerp(biquad_coeff_t a, biquad_coeff_t b, float t) {
  return biquad_coeff_add(a, biquad_coeff_mul(biquad_coeff_diff(b, a), t));
}
static inline float biquad_process_sample(biquad_t *b, const biquad_coeff_t *c, float x) {
  float y = c->fb0 * x + b->fz1;
  b->fz1 = c->fb1 * x - c->fa1 * y + b->fz2;
  b->fz2 = c->fb2 * x - c->fa2 * y;
  return y;
}

/*
## Fixed-Size FFT Helpers

`fft_512(...)` restores Plinky's old 512-sample real FFT helper for panel DSP code.

The input `x` must be 512 mono samples that have already been windowed by the caller. The function reuses both `x` and `y` as
working memory, destroys the original contents of `x`, and always returns `y` as the final output buffer.

The output keeps the historical packing and scaling:

  - for bins `k = 1..255`, `y[2*k + 0]` / `y[2*k + 1]` hold `2 * real` / `2 * imag`
  - `y[0]` holds `2 * DC`
  - `y[1]` is always `0`
  - the Nyquist bin (`k = 256`) is not stored separately by this helper

`get_fft_512_window()` returns the same 512-point cosine table used by the FFT's final unpacking step. The old pre-windowing
shape used with this FFT is `1.0f - get_fft_512_window()[i]`.
*/
float *fft_512(float x[512], float y[512]);
const float *get_fft_512_window(void);

/*
## LED And Colour Helpers

The same 16x16 grid is both the display and the main touch surface. Colours are packed into Plinky's LED format. You can work
directly with explicit RGB values, or use the fixed palette helpers for compact, readable panel code.
*/

#define LED_RGB(r, g, b) (uint32_t)(((g) << 24) | ((r) << 16) | ((b) << 8))
#define PINK LED_RGB(20, 0, 31)
#define PURPLE LED_RGB(10, 0, 31)
#define RED LED_RGB(31, 0, 0)
#define ORANGE LED_RGB(31, 13, 0)
#define YELLOW LED_RGB(31, 31, 1)
#define GREEN LED_RGB(0, 31, 0)
#define CYAN LED_RGB(0, 31, 31)
#define BLUE LED_RGB(0, 0, 31)
#define TEAL LED_RGB(0, 16, 31)
#define WHITE LED_RGB(15, 15, 15)
#define BLACK 0

#define MOD_SRC_VISUAL_SOURCE_COUNT 5u
static const uint32_t mod_src_colors[MOD_SRC_VISUAL_SOURCE_COUNT] = {YELLOW, TEAL, RED, GREEN, WHITE};
static const char mod_src_names[MOD_SRC_VISUAL_SOURCE_COUNT] = {'A', 'B', 'X', 'Y', 'P'};
static inline uint32_t get_mod_src_color(int mod_source) {
  return ((unsigned)mod_source < MOD_SRC_VISUAL_SOURCE_COUNT) ? mod_src_colors[mod_source] : WHITE;
}
static inline char get_mod_src_name(int mod_source) {
  return ((unsigned)mod_source < MOD_SRC_VISUAL_SOURCE_COUNT) ? mod_src_names[mod_source] : '?';
}

// replicating the middle brightness row from the palette.h file
#define RAINBOW0 LED_RGB(20, 0, 31) // pink
#define RAINBOW1 LED_RGB(31, 0, 0)  // red
#define RAINBOW2 LED_RGB(31, 6, 0)  // red-orange
#define RAINBOW3 LED_RGB(31, 20, 0) // orange
#define RAINBOW4 LED_RGB(31, 31, 1) // yellow
#define RAINBOW5 LED_RGB(31, 31, 3)
#define RAINBOW6 LED_RGB(10, 31, 1)
#define RAINBOW7 LED_RGB(0, 31, 0) // green
#define RAINBOW8 LED_RGB(0, 31, 20)
#define RAINBOW9 LED_RGB(0, 31, 31) // teal
#define RAINBOW10 LED_RGB(0, 15, 31)
#define RAINBOW11 LED_RGB(0, 0, 31) // blue
#define RAINBOW12 LED_RGB(3, 0, 31)
#define RAINBOW13 LED_RGB(10, 0, 31)
#define RAINBOW14 LED_RGB(10, 3, 31)
#define RAINBOW15 LED_RGB(10, 10, 20)

// you can combine colors with these like BRIGHTEST(PINK) etc
#define BRIGHTEST(rgb) ((rgb) << 2)
#define BRIGHTER(rgb) ((rgb) << 1)
#define DIMMER(rgb) ((rgb & 0xfefefe00) >> 1)
#define DIMMEST(rgb) (((rgb) & 0xfcfcfc00) >> 2)
#define DIMMESTEST(rgb) (((rgb) & 0xf8f8f800) >> 3)

// Colour arithmetic helpers are declared here for discovery; the tiny inline implementations are tucked into a collapsible block.
static inline uint32_t fade_col(uint32_t rgb, int brightness_q8);
static inline uint32_t add_col(uint32_t x, uint32_t y);
static inline uint32_t maxcol(uint32_t x, uint32_t y);
static inline uint32_t lerp_col(uint32_t y, uint32_t x, int t);

static inline uint32_t fade_col(uint32_t rgb, int brightness_q8) {
  int r = mini(255, (((rgb >> 16) & 0xff) * brightness_q8) >> 8);
  int g = mini(255, (((rgb >> 24) & 0xff) * brightness_q8) >> 8);
  int b = mini(255, (((rgb >> 8) & 0xff) * brightness_q8) >> 8);
  return LED_RGB(r, g, b);
}
static inline uint32_t add_col(uint32_t x, uint32_t y) {
  int r = mini(255, (((x >> 16) & 0xff) + ((y >> 16) & 0xff)));
  int g = mini(255, (((x >> 24) & 0xff) + ((y >> 24) & 0xff)));
  int b = mini(255, (((x >> 8) & 0xff) + ((y >> 8) & 0xff)));
  return LED_RGB(r, g, b);
}

static inline uint32_t maxcol(uint32_t x, uint32_t y) {
  int r = maxi((int)((x >> 16) & 0xff), (int)((y >> 16) & 0xff));
  int g = maxi((int)((x >> 24) & 0xff), (int)((y >> 24) & 0xff));
  int b = maxi((int)((x >> 8) & 0xff), (int)((y >> 8) & 0xff));
  return LED_RGB(r, g, b);
}

static inline uint32_t lerp_col(uint32_t y, uint32_t x, int t) {
  int r = clampi((((x >> 16) & 0xff) * t + ((y >> 16) & 0xff) * (256 - t)) >> 8, 0, 255);
  int g = clampi((((x >> 24) & 0xff) * t + ((y >> 24) & 0xff) * (256 - t)) >> 8, 0, 255);
  int b = clampi((((x >> 8) & 0xff) * t + ((y >> 8) & 0xff) * (256 - t)) >> 8, 0, 255);
  return LED_RGB(r, g, b);
}

extern const uint32_t palette[16][16]; // a palette of 16 brightnesses of 16 rainbow colours. so you can do rgbs[i] =
                                       // palette[brightnesss][hue] for example


// maps a 16-step hue thru the standard palette with a default brightness of 8
static inline uint32_t palette_hue_to_col(uint8_t hue_q4, int brightness_q3 BLOCKS_LL_DEFAULT_ARG(8)) {
  return palette[brightness_q3 & 15][hue_q4 & 15];
}

// maps a 256-step hue thru 3 sinewave type hue.
uint32_t hue_q8_to_col(uint8_t hue_q8, int brightness_q8);


enum { LED_RGBS_COUNT = 256 };
#define LED_RGBS_SIZE_BYTES (LED_RGBS_COUNT * sizeof(uint32_t))

extern uint32_t *rgbs;
extern uint8_t display_flip;
extern uint32_t frame_count; // led frame count
extern int scroll_y;         // global vertical logical scroll offset in LEDs

static inline bool is_y_visible(int y1, int y2) {
  return (y1<16+scroll_y && y2>scroll_y);
}

uint32_t get_led(int x, int y);

static inline void leds_clear_tophalf() { memset(rgbs, 0, LED_RGBS_SIZE_BYTES / 2); }
void leds_rectangle(int x1, int y1, int x2, int y2, uint32_t rgb15); // draw a rectangle of leds

static inline void leds_set_all(uint32_t rgb15) {
  for (int i = 0; i < LED_RGBS_COUNT; ++i)
    rgbs[i] = rgb15;
}
enum {
  FONT_4,
  FONT_4_BOLD,
  FONT_5,
};

static inline void leds_vline(int x1, int y1, int y2, uint32_t rgb15) { leds_rectangle(x1, y1, x1 + 1, y2, rgb15); }

int leds_string_width(const char *c, uint8_t fontidx);
